024519,002150:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
024520,002151: 
024521,002152:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
024522,002153:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
024523,002154:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024524,002155:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
024525,002156:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
024526,002157:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024527,002158:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
024528,002159:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
024529,002160:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
024530,002161:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
024531,002162:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
024532,002163:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
024533,002164:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
024534,002165:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
024535,002166:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
024536,002167:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
024537,002168:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
024538,002169:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
024539,002170:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
024540,002171:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
024541,002172:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024542,002173: 
024543,002174:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024544,002175:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
024545,002176: 
024546,002177:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024547,002178:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
024548,002179: 
024549,002180:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024550,002181:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR, WAITLIST
024551,002182: 
024552,002183:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024553,002184:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES
024554,002185:

024556,002187:

024691,002322:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024692,002323: 
024693,002324:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024694,002325:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024695,002326:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024696,002327:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024697,002328:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024698,002329:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024699,002330:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024700,002331:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024701,002332:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024702,002333:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024703,002334:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024704,002335:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024705,002336:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024706,002337:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024707,002338:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024708,002339:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024709,002340:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024710,002341:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024711,002342:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024712,002343:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024713,002344:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024714,002345:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024715,002346:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024716,002347:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024717,002348:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024718,002349:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024719,002350: 
024720,002351:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024721,002352:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024722,002353:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024723,002354:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024724,002355: 
024725,002356:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024726,002357:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024727,002358: 
024728,002359:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024729,002360:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024730,002361: 
024731,002362:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024732,002363: 
024733,002364:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024734,002365:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024735,002366: 
024736,002367:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024737,002368:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024738,002369:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024739,002370: 
024740,002371: 25,2564           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

024784,002415:

Page 563 

024786,002417:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024787,002418: 
024788,002419:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024789,002420:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024790,002421:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024791,002422:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024792,002423:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024793,002424:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024794,002425:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024795,002426:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024796,002427:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024797,002428:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
024798,002429:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024799,002430:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024800,002431:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
024801,002432:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024802,002433:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024803,002434:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024804,002435:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024805,002436:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024806,002437:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024807,002438:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024808,002439:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024809,002440:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024810,002441:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024811,002442:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024812,002443:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024813,002444:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024814,002445:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024815,002446:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024816,002447:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024817,002448:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024818,002449:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024819,002450:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024820,002451:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024821,002452:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024822,002453:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024823,002454:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024824,002455:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024825,002456:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024826,002457: 
024827,002458:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024828,002459:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024829,002460: 
024830,002461:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024831,002462:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024832,002463:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024833,002464: 
024834,002465:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024835,002466:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
024836,002467:

025118,002749:                                                                                                  #  RADAR RUPT READER (R20)
025119,002750: 
025120,002751:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE, WHICH IS INITIATED BY A RADAR RUPT, PROCESSES THE RADAR DATA AND UPDATES THE APPROPRIATE
025121,002752:                                                                                                  #  DSKY LIGHTS.

025763,003394:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025764,003395:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025765,003396: 
025766,003397: 
025767,003398:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025768,003399: 
025769,003400:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025770,003401:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025771,003402:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025772,003403: 
025773,003404:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025774,003405: 
025775,003406: 
025776,003407:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025777,003408: 
025778,003409: 
025779,003410:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025780,003411: 
025781,003412:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT    LPS20.1
025782,003413:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025783,003414:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025784,003415:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025785,003416:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025786,003417: 
025787,003418: 
025788,003419:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025789,003420: 
025790,003421:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025791,003422:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025792,003423: 
025793,003424: 
025794,003425:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025795,003426:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025796,003427: 
025797,003428: 
025798,003429:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025799,003430:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025800,003431: 
025801,003432:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025802,003433: 
025803,003434:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025804,003435:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025805,003436:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025806,003437:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
025807,003438:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
025808,003439: 
025809,003440: 
025810,003441:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025811,003442: 
025812,003443:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 588 

025814,003445:                                                                                                  #      1)RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
025815,003446:                                                                                                  #      2)RR RANGE RATE,SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
025816,003447: 
025817,003448:                                                                                                  #     THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX,CDUY,CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2

026031,003662:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
026032,003663:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
026033,003664:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
026034,003665: 
026035,003666:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026036,003667: 
026037,003668:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
026038,003669:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
026039,003670:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
026040,003671: 
026041,003672:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
026042,003673:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
026043,003674:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
026044,003675:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
026045,003676:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
026046,003677:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
026047,003678:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
026048,003679: 
026049,003680: 
026050,003681:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026051,003682:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
026052,003683:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
026053,003684: 
026054,003685:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026055,003686:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026056,003687:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026057,003688:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026058,003689:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026059,003690:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026060,003691: 
026061,003692: 
026062,003693:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026063,003694:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
026064,003695:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
026065,003696:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
026066,003697:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
026067,003698:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
026068,003699:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
026069,003700:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
026070,003701:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
026071,003702:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
026072,003703:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
026073,003704:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
026074,003705:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
026075,003706:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
026076,003707:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
026077,003708: 
026078,003709:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026079,003710:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
026080,003711:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

026082,003713:                                                                                                  #   ULC,RXZ,SINTHETA,LGRET,RDRET,BVECTOR,W.IND,X78T

026471,004102: 26,3205           50644                                    R22LEM93                              
026472,004103:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026473,004104: 
026474,004105:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
026475,004106:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
026476,004107:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
026477,004108: 
026478,004109:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026479,004110:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
026480,004111:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
026481,004112: 
026482,004113:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026483,004114:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026484,004115:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026485,004116:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026486,004117:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026487,004118:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026488,004119:

Page 603 

026490,004121:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026491,004122:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
026492,004123:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
026493,004124:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
026494,004125:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
026495,004126:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
026496,004127:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
026497,004128: 
026498,004129:

026703,004334:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
026704,004335:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
026705,004336: 
026706,004337: 
026707,004338:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026708,004339: 
026709,004340:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
026710,004341:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
026711,004342:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
026712,004343:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
026713,004344: 
026714,004345: 
026715,004346:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026716,004347: 
026717,004348: 
026718,004349:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026719,004350: 
026720,004351:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026721,004352:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026722,004353:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026723,004354:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026724,004355:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026725,004356: 
026726,004357: 
026727,004358:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -  TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026728,004359: 
026729,004360: 
026730,004361:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026731,004362: 
026732,004363:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026733,004364:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026734,004365:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026735,004366: 
026736,004367:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026737,004368:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026738,004369:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026739,004370:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026740,004371: 
026741,004372:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026742,004373:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026743,004374:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026744,004375:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026745,004376:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026746,004377: 
026747,004378: 
026748,004379: 26,3441                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24
